.contains-task-list&#123;padding-left:0&#125;.markdown-body .task-list-item&#123;list-style:none&#125;@media (max-width:720px)&#123;.markdown-body h1&#123;font-size:24px&#125;.markdown-body h2&#123;font-size:20px&#125;.markdown-body h3&#123;font-size:18px&#125;&#125;</style><h2 data-id="heading-0">贝塞尔曲线的定义及推导过程</h2>
<p>　　贝塞尔曲线于1962年，由法国工程师皮埃尔·贝兹（Pierre Bézier）所广泛发表，他运用贝塞尔曲线来为汽车的主体进行设计。贝塞尔曲线最初由保尔·德·卡斯特里奥于1959年运用德卡斯特里奥算法开发，以稳定数值的方法求出贝塞尔曲线。贝塞尔曲线由ｎ个控制点对应着ｎ－１阶的贝塞尔曲线，并且可以通过<code>递归</code>的方式来绘制。</p>
<p>　　下面先给出n阶贝塞尔曲线的公式</p>
<p><img src="https://p6-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/29f38d3ba8cd4d6d9e525f47e9642187~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-watermark.image" alt="n阶.svg" loading="lazy" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p>
<h3 data-id="heading-1">一阶贝塞尔曲线</h3>
<p><img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/df6d7fddddfc45e3b3519ffab16275bc~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-watermark.image" alt="一阶动画.gif" loading="lazy" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p>
<p>　　设定图中运动的点为<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.61508em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span></span></span></span></span>为运动时间，<span class="math separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t∈(0,1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.65418em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span></span>)，可得如下公式</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable <h3 data-id="heading-2">二阶贝塞尔曲线</h3>
<p><img src="https://p1-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/569560be661647cea7180a7806356dc8~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-watermark.image" alt="二阶动画.gif" loading="lazy" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p>

<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>t</mi><mo </ol>
<p>　　由公式（1）可得</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable fence="true">(</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>t</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mi>t</mi></mrow></mtd><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mtext>(2)</mtext></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_a=P_0+\left(P_1-P_0\right)t=\left(1-t\right)P_0+P_1t \tag &#123;2&#125;</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.30110799999999993em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span <p>　　将公式（2）和公式（3）代入公式（4）可得</p>

mathnormal mtight">e</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.33610799999999996em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" mathnormal mtight">d</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" <li><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>t</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.61508em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span></span></span></span></span>从0变化到1的过程中，所有<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2805559999999999em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>点就组成了三阶贝塞尔曲线。</li>
</ol>
<p>　　由之前的公式可得：</p>

<p>　　将上述公式带入<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>t</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_t</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2805559999999999em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">t</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>可得</p>

style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8641079999999999em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;">)</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8641079999999999em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.30110799999999993em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">3</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:1em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;">(</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;">)</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:4.478016em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<h3 data-id="heading-4">递归性质</h3>
<p>　　仔细观察上述的构造过程，经过第5步变化之后，三阶贝塞尔曲线的求解变成了对以<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>a</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.151392em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">a</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>为起点，<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>c</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_c</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.151392em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">c</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>为终点，<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>b</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.33610799999999996em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">b</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>为控制点的二阶贝塞尔曲线方程的求解。</p>
<p>　　首先，有四个控制点；<br>
四个控制点形成三个线段，每个线段上有一个点在运动，于是得到三个点；<br>
三个控制点形成两个线段，每个线段上有一个点在运动，于是得到两个点；<br>
两个点形成一个线段，这个线段上有一个点在运动，于是得到一个点；<br>
最后一个点的运动轨迹便构成了贝塞尔曲线！</p>
<p>　　我们发现，实际上是每轮都是 n 个点，形成 n-1 条线段，每个线段上有一个点在运动，那么就只关注这 n-1 个点，循环往复。最终只剩一个点时，它的轨迹便是结果。</p>
<p>这就是我们前面提到的贝塞尔曲线的递归性质。</p>
<p>　　通过对上面贝塞尔曲线的定义及推导过程的阅读，我们对贝塞尔曲线是什么以及如何获得相应阶数的曲线公式有了初步的认识，那么在日常开发中我们如何定义并使用贝塞尔曲线呢？<code>UIBezierPath</code> 是<code>UIKit</code>中的一个关于图形绘制的类，是对<code>CGPathRef</code>的封装，可以方便的让我们画出 矩形、椭圆或者直线和曲线的组合形状。下面我们简单介绍一下<code>UIBezierPath</code>的常用api。</p>
<h3 data-id="heading-5">UIBezierPath</h3>
<p>　<code>UIBezierPath</code>用于定义一个直线和曲线组合而成的路径，并且可以在自定义视图中渲染该路径。</p>
<h4 data-id="heading-6">常用api</h4>
<p>一、创建<code>UIBezierPath</code>.</p>
<pre><code class="hljs language-objc copyable" lang="objc"><span class="hljs-comment">//创建并返回一个新的bezierPath对象</span>
+ (<span class="hljs-keyword">instancetype</span>)bezierPath;

<span class="hljs-comment">//通过一个矩形rect创建并返回一个矩形bezierPath对象</span>
+ (<span class="hljs-keyword">instancetype</span>)bezierPathWithRect:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGRect</span>)rect;

<span class="hljs-comment">//通过一个矩形rect创建并返回一个与该矩形内接的椭圆bezierPath对象</span>
+ (<span class="hljs-keyword">instancetype</span>)bezierPathWithOvalInRect:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGRect</span>)rect;

<span class="hljs-comment">//创建一个圆角矩形路径，以CGRect为大小，以cornerRadius为圆角半径</span>
+ (<span class="hljs-keyword">instancetype</span>)bezierPathWithRoundedRect:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGRect</span>)rect cornerRadius:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span>)cornerRadius;

<span class="hljs-comment">//创建一个圆角矩形路径，以CGRect为大小，以corners选择圆角位置，以cornerRadii为圆角半径</span>
+ (<span class="hljs-keyword">instancetype</span>)bezierPathWithRoundedRect:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGRect</span>)rect byRoundingCorners:(<span class="hljs-built_in">UIRectCorner</span>)corners cornerRadii:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGSize</span>)cornerRadii;

<span class="hljs-comment">//创建一个圆弧路径，以center为圆弧圆心，radius为圆弧半径，startAngle为圆弧起始角度，endAngle为圆弧终止角度，clockwise为路径绘制方向，YES：顺时针绘制</span>
+ (<span class="hljs-keyword">instancetype</span>)bezierPathWithArcCenter:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span>)center radius:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span>)radius startAngle:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span>)startAngle endAngle:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span>)endAngle clockwise:(<span class="hljs-built_in">BOOL</span>)clockwise;

<span class="hljs-comment">//通过一个已存在的路径，返回一个该路径的反转路径</span>
- (<span class="hljs-built_in">UIBezierPath</span> *)bezierPathByReversingPath;

<p>二、绘制路径</p>
<pre><code class="hljs language-objc copyable" lang="objc"><span class="hljs-comment">//移动path的currentPoint到指定的位置</span>

<h3 data-id="heading-7">定义了path之后如何绘制到屏幕上？</h3>
<ol>
<li>在UIView的<code>- (void)drawRect:(CGRect)rect</code>方法里面绘制图形</li>
<li>使用CAShapeLayer</li>
</ol>
<p><code>CAShapeLayer</code>和<code>drawRect</code>比较：</p>
<ul>
<li>CAShapeLayer：属于CoreAnimation框架，通过GPU来渲染图形，节省性能，高效使用内存。</li>
<li>drawRect：属于Core Graphics框架，占用大量CPU，耗费性能。</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-id="heading-8">CAShapeLayer</h3>
<p>　　<code>CAShapeLayer</code>继承自<code>CALayer</code>。<code>CAShapeLayer</code>属于<code>CoreAnimation</code>框架，通过GPU来渲染图形，节省性能。动画渲染直接提交给手机GPU，高效使用内存。 每个<code>CAShapeLayer</code>对象都代表着将要被渲染到屏幕上的一个任意的形状（shape）。具体的形状由其path（类型为<code>CGPathRef</code>）属性指定。 普通的<code>CALayer</code>是矩形，需要<code>frame</code>属性。<code>CAShapeLayer</code>初始化时也需要指定<code>frame</code>值，但它本身没有形状，它的形状来源于其属性path 。<code>CAShapeLayer</code>中shape需要形状才能生效。<code>UIBezierPath</code>可以为其提供绘制形状的path。</p>
<h3 data-id="heading-9">常用api</h3>
<pre><code class="hljs language-objc copyable" lang="objc"><span class="hljs-comment">//图层渲染的路径 Animatable，对path进行动画时，要注意保证前后两个path拥有相同数量的控制点</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">nullable</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPathRef</span> path;

<span class="hljs-comment">//图层路径颜色</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">nullable</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">CGColorRef</span> strokeColor;

<span class="hljs-comment">//路径渲染的起止相对位置，取值在[0,1]之间，可动画</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> strokeStart;
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> strokeEnd;

<span class="hljs-comment">//开始绘制位置在虚线长度中的位置</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> lineDashPhase;

<span class="hljs-comment">//虚线的规格，数组定义了实线和空格的宽度</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">nullable</span>, <span class="hljs-keyword">copy</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">NSArray</span><<span class="hljs-built_in">NSNumber</span> *> *lineDashPattern;

<span class="hljs-comment">//线宽，意义同UIBezierPath</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> lineWidth;

<span class="hljs-comment">//起点和终点样式，意义同UIBezierPath</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">copy</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">CAShapeLayerLineCap</span> lineCap;

<span class="hljs-comment">//连接点样式，意义同UIBezierPath</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@property</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">copy</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">CAShapeLayerLineJoin</span> lineJoin;
<span class="copy-code-btn">复制代码</span></code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-10">举个例子</h2>
<p><img src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/c9611ecb1d6f4f2db5fc0c2d0b630e1a~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-watermark.image" alt="wavegif2.gif" loading="lazy" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p>
<p><img src="https://p6-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/485c91c32e0648879442e981b037c3b9~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-watermark.image" alt="示意图2.png" loading="lazy" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">
　　下面我们将用二阶和三阶贝塞尔曲线实现上面的波浪动图效果，如上示意图所示，将波浪曲线进行分解，通过绘制两个相同的完整的“正弦波”，然后不停的将曲线向左侧移动和复位，来达到波浪起伏的效果。</p>
<h3 data-id="heading-11">二阶实现</h3>
<pre><code class="hljs language-objc copyable" lang="objc"><span class="hljs-comment">// p0p1，p1p2，p2p3，p3p4为4条二阶曲线，c1，c2，c3，c4为其相应二阶贝塞尔曲线的控制点</span>

- (<span class="hljs-keyword">void</span>)p_creatWavePath &#123;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> waterHeight = <span class="hljs-number">300.</span>f;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> waveWidth = <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.view.frame.size.width / <span class="hljs-number">2.</span>f;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> waveControlHeight = <span class="hljs-number">50.</span>f;
    
    <span class="hljs-built_in">UIBezierPath</span> *wavePath = [<span class="hljs-built_in">UIBezierPath</span> bezierPath];
    [wavePath moveToPoint:<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)];
    [wavePath addLineToPoint:<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight)];
    
    <span class="hljs-comment">// 计算起点和控制点</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> waveHeight = <span class="hljs-number">20.</span>f;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p0 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p1 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p2 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p3 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">3</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p4 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">4</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c1 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">1</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight - waveControlHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c2 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">3</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight + waveControlHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c3 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">5</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight - waveControlHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c4 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">7</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight + waveControlHeight);
    [wavePath addQuadCurveToPoint:p1 controlPoint:c1];
    [wavePath addQuadCurveToPoint:p2 controlPoint:c2];
    [wavePath addQuadCurveToPoint:p3 controlPoint:c3];
    [wavePath addQuadCurveToPoint:p4 controlPoint:c4];
    
    [wavePath addLineToPoint:<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">4</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)];
    [wavePath closePath];
    <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveLayer.path = wavePath.CGPath;
    <span class="hljs-comment">// 累加曲线的向左的偏移量</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX = (<span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX + <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveStepX) % (<span class="hljs-built_in">NSInteger</span>)(<span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.view.frame.size.width);
&#125;

<span class="copy-code-btn">复制代码</span></code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-12">三阶实现</h2>
<pre><code class="hljs language-objc copyable" lang="objc"><span class="hljs-comment">// p0p1p2，p2p3p4为两条三阶阶曲线，c1和c2，c3和c4为其相应三阶贝塞尔曲线的控制点</span>

- (<span class="hljs-keyword">void</span>)p_creatWavePath &#123;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> waterHeight = <span class="hljs-number">300.</span>f;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> waveWidth = <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.view.frame.size.width / <span class="hljs-number">2.</span>f;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> waveControlHeight = <span class="hljs-number">50.</span>f;
    
    <span class="hljs-built_in">UIBezierPath</span> *wavePath = [<span class="hljs-built_in">UIBezierPath</span> bezierPath];
    [wavePath moveToPoint:<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)];
    [wavePath addLineToPoint:<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight)];
    
    <span class="hljs-comment">// 计算起点和控制点</span>
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p2 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p4 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">4</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c1 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth  * <span class="hljs-number">1</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight - waveControlHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c2 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">3</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight + waveControlHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c3 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">5</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight - waveControlHeight);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> c4 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">7</span> / <span class="hljs-number">2</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, waterHeight + waveControlHeight);
    [wavePath addCurveToPoint:p2 controlPoint1:c1 controlPoint2:c2];
    [wavePath addCurveToPoint:p4 controlPoint1:c3 controlPoint2:c4];
    
    [wavePath addLineToPoint:<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointMake</span>(waveWidth * <span class="hljs-number">4</span> - <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>)];
    [wavePath closePath];
    <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveLayer.path = wavePath.CGPath;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX = (<span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveOffsetX + <span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.waveStepX) % (<span class="hljs-built_in">NSInteger</span>)(<span class="hljs-keyword">self</span>.view.frame.size.width);
&#125;
<span class="copy-code-btn">复制代码</span></code></pre>
<h2 data-id="heading-13">反推控制点</h2>
<p>　　由之前的介绍可知，要绘制一条贝塞尔曲线，除了起点和终点外，还必须要知道相应数量的控制点。但在日常开发中我们并不是总能知道控制点，取而代之的是一些曲线经过的点，这个时候要怎么办呢？下面以三阶曲线为例，推导控制点的计算过程</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>t</mi><mo \left(1-t\right)^3P_0+3t\left(1-t\right)^2P_1+3t^2\left(1-t\right)P_2+t^3P_3 \quad\quad t\in\left(0,1\right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span <p>　　移动方程式可得：</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mn>3</mn><mi>t</mi><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>t</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><mn>3</mn><msup><mi>t</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>t</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>t</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>t</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mn>3</mn></msup><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo>−</mo><msup><mi>t</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mspace width="1em"></mspace></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">3t\left(1-t\right)^2P_1+3t^2\left(1-t\right)P_2 = P_t - \left(1-t\right)^3P_0 - t^3P_3 \quad\quad</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.204008em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;">(</span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;">)</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.954008em;"><span style="top:-3.2029em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.30110799999999993em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.1141079999999999em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">3</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8641079999999999em;"><span <p>　　设<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math <div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable <p>　　同理将t=3/4时的点<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>b</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.33610799999999996em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">b</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>带入公式可得：</p>

<p>　　设<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math <div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable <p>　　将公式(5)和公式(6)代入化简可得：</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>72</mn><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mn>3</mn><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>b</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>a</mi></msub><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>72</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">P_1=\left(3P_a-P_b\right)/72 \\ P_2=\left(3P_b-P_a\right)/72</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.30110799999999993em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.151392em;"><span style="top:-2.5500000000000003em;margin-left:-0.13889em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord">7</span><span class="mord">2</span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>　　下面是上述例子中控制点求解的函数实现</p>
<pre><code class="hljs language-objc copyable" lang="objc"><span class="hljs-comment">// 三阶曲线求控制点</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// p0：起点，p3：终点，pa：t=t1时曲线上的点，pb：t=t2时曲线上的点</span>
- (<span class="hljs-built_in">NSArray</span><<span class="hljs-built_in">NSValue</span> *> *)p_calculateControlPointsWithPoint0:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span>)p0 pointA:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span>)pa t1:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span>)t1 pointB:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span>)pb t2:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span>)t2 point3:(<span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span>)p3 &#123;
    <span class="hljs-comment">// ax + by = c</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">// dx + ey = f</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">// x = (b * f - c * e) / (b * d - a * e)</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">// y = (c * d - a * f) / (b * d - a * e)</span>
    
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> fa = <span class="hljs-number">3</span> * t1 * pow((<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t1), <span class="hljs-number">2</span>);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> fb = <span class="hljs-number">3</span> * (<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t1) * pow(t1, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> fd = <span class="hljs-number">3</span> * t2 * pow((<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t2), <span class="hljs-number">2</span>);
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> fe = <span class="hljs-number">3</span> * (<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t2) * pow(t2, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>);

    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> fcx = pa.x - pow((<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t1), <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p0.x - pow(t1, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p3.x;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> fcy = pa.y - pow((<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t1), <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p0.y - pow(t1, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p3.y;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> ffx = pb.x - pow((<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t2), <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p0.x - pow(t2, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p3.x;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGFloat</span> ffy = pb.y - pow((<span class="hljs-number">1</span> - t2), <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p0.y - pow(t2, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>) * p3.y;
    
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p1 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointZero</span>;
    <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPoint</span> p2 = <span class="hljs-built_in">CGPointZero</span>;
    p1.x = (fb * fcx - ffx * fe) / (fb * fd - fa * fe);
    p1.y = (fb * fcy - ffy * fe) / (fb * fd - fa * fe);
    p2.x = (fd * fcx - ffx * fa) / (fb * fd - fa * fe);
    p2.y = (fd * fcy - ffy * fa) / (fb * fd - fa * fe);
    
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> @[[<span class="hljs-built_in">NSValue</span> valueWithCGPoint:p1], [<span class="hljs-built_in">NSValue</span> valueWithCGPoint:p2]];
&#125;
<span class="copy-code-btn">复制代码</span></code></pre>
